let currentProblem = null; let filteredProblems = []; const SYMBOL_MAP = { '∆í': '√∑', '‚Äö': '√ó', '√à': '‚àö', '»à': '‚àö', '¬≥‚àö': '‚àõ', '¬∏': '|', '': '', '': '', ' ': ' ' }; document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initApp); function initApp(){ if(typeof PROBLEMS_DATA === 'undefined' || !PROBLEMS_DATA.length){ showError('Failed to load embedded problem data'); return; } allProblems = PROBLEMS_DATA.map((p, i) => ({ ...p, id: i, cleaned: false, answer: '', cleanedQuestion: p.q || '' })); loadSavedProgress(); populateFilters(); updateStats(); applyFilters(); if(filteredProblems.length > 0) selectProblem(filteredProblems[0]); else showEmptyEditor(); } function loadSavedProgress(){ try { const saved = localStorage.getItem('uilCleanupProgress'); if(saved){ const data = JSON.parse(saved); data.forEach(sp => { const p = allProblems.find(x => x.id === sp.id); if(p){ p.cleaned = sp.cleaned || false; p.answer = sp.answer || ''; p.cleanedQuestion = sp.cleanedQuestion || p.q; p.t = sp.t || p.t; } }); } } catch(e){ console.error('Error loading progress:', e); } } function populateFilters(){ const years = [...new Set(allProblems.map(p => p.year))].sort(); const sel = document.getElementById('filter-year'); years.forEach(y => { const opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = y; opt.textContent = y; sel.appendChild(opt); }); } function updateStats(){ const cleaned = allProblems.filter(p => p.cleaned).length; const total = allProblems.length; document.getElementById('total-count').textContent = total; document.getElementById('cleaned-count').textContent = cleaned; document.getElementById('remaining-count').textContent = total - cleaned; document.getElementById('percent-done').textContent = ((cleaned/total)*100).toFixed(1) + '%'; document.getElementById('progress-fill').style.width = ((cleaned/total)*100) + '%'; } function applyFilters(){ const year = document.getElementById('filter-year').value; const test = document.getElementById('filter-test').value; const status = document.getElementById('filter-status').value; const numMin = parseInt(document.getElementById('filter-num-min').value) || 1; const numMax = parseInt(document.getElementById('filter-num-max').value) || 80; filteredProblems = allProblems.filter(p => { if(year && p.year !== year) return false; if(test && p.test !== test) return false; if(status === 'dirty' && p.cleaned) return false; if(status === 'clean' && !p.cleaned) return false; if(status === 'starred' && !p.starred) return false; if(p.num < numMin || p.num > numMax) return false; return true; }); renderProblemList(); } function renderProblemList(){ const container = document.getElementById('problem-list-items'); if(!filteredProblems.length){ container.innerHTML = '
No problems match filters
'; return; } container.innerHTML = filteredProblems.map(p => `
${p.starred ? '‚≠ê ' : ''}#${p.num} ${p.year} ${p.test} ${p.cleaned ? '‚úì' : '‚úó'}
${(p.cleanedQuestion || p.q || '').substring(0, 50)}...
`).join(''); } function selectProblemById(id){ const p = allProblems.find(x => x.id === id); if(p) selectProblem(p); } function selectProblem(p){ currentProblem = p; renderProblemList(); renderEditor(p); } function renderEditor(p){ document.getElementById('editor-content').innerHTML = `
${p.starred ? '‚≠ê ' : ''}Problem #${p.num} (${p.year} Test ${p.test})

üîß Common Symbol Replacements:

∆í ‚Üí √∑
‚Äö ‚Üí √ó
√à ‚Üí ‚àö
q ‚Üí ‚àí
¬∏ ‚Üí |
üí° Tip: For fractions use 1/2, for mixed numbers use 2 1/2
`; } function showEmptyEditor(){ document.getElementById('editor-content').innerHTML = `

üéØ No Problem Selected

Select a problem from the list on the left to start cleaning!

üí° Tip: Filter to "Starred Only" to focus on the most important problems first.

`; } function showError(msg){ document.getElementById('editor-content').innerHTML = `

‚ö†Ô∏è Error

${msg}

`; } function autoReplace(){ const textarea = document.getElementById('cleaned-question'); let text = textarea.value; Object.entries(SYMBOL_MAP).forEach(([bad, good]) => { text = text.split(bad).join(good); }); text = text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(); textarea.value = text; textarea.focus(); } function insertSymbol(sym){ const textarea = document.getElementById('cleaned-question'); const start = textarea.selectionStart; const end = textarea.selectionEnd; const text = textarea.value; textarea.value = text.substring(0, start) + sym + text.substring(end); textarea.focus(); textarea.setSelectionRange(start + sym.length, start + sym.length); } function saveProblem(){ const cleanedQ = document.getElementById('cleaned-question').value.trim(); const answer = document.getElementById('answer').value.trim(); const topic = document.getElementById('topic').value; if(!cleanedQ){ showMessage('‚ö†Ô∏è Please enter a cleaned question', 'error'); return; } currentProblem.cleanedQuestion = cleanedQ; currentProblem.answer = answer; currentProblem.t = topic; currentProblem.cleaned = true; saveToLocalStorage(); updateStats(); showMessage('‚úÖ Saved successfully!', 'success'); setTimeout(() => { const idx = filteredProblems.findIndex(p => p.id === currentProblem.id); if(idx < filteredProblems.length - 1){ selectProblem(filteredProblems[idx + 1]); } else { showMessage('üéâ All filtered problems completed!', 'success'); } }, 600); } function skipProblem(){ const idx = filteredProblems.findIndex(p => p.id === currentProblem.id); if(idx < filteredProblems.length - 1){ selectProblem(filteredProblems[idx + 1]); } } function saveToLocalStorage(){ const progress = allProblems.map(p => ({ id: p.id, cleaned: p.cleaned, cleanedQuestion: p.cleanedQuestion, answer: p.answer, t: p.t })); localStorage.setItem('uilCleanupProgress', JSON.stringify(progress)); } function downloadProgress(){ const cleaned = allProblems.filter(p => p.cleaned).map(p => ({ num: p.num, q: p.cleanedQuestion, a: p.answer, t: p.t, year: p.year, test: p.test, starred: p.starred, source: p.source })); const data = { exported: new Date().toISOString(), total: allProblems.length, cleaned: cleaned.length, problems: cleaned }; const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], {type: 'application/json'}); const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob); const a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = url; a.download = `uil-cleaned-problems-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json`; a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(url); showMessage(`üíæ Downloaded ${cleaned.length} cleaned problems`, 'success'); } function uploadProgress(){ document.getElementById('upload-input').click(); } function handleUpload(evt){ const file = evt.target.files[0]; if(!file) return; const reader = new FileReader(); reader.onload = e => { try { const data = JSON.parse(e.target.result); const imported = data.problems || data; imported.forEach(imp => { const p = allProblems.find(x => x.num === imp.num && x.year === imp.year && x.test === imp.test); if(p){ p.cleanedQuestion = imp.q; p.answer = imp.a; p.t = imp.t; p.cleaned = true; } }); saveToLocalStorage(); updateStats(); applyFilters(); showMessage(`‚úÖ Imported ${imported.length} cleaned problems`, 'success'); } catch(err){ showMessage('‚ö†Ô∏è Error importing file: ' + err.message, 'error'); } }; reader.readAsText(file); } function clearProgress(){ if(!confirm('‚ö†Ô∏è Are you sure you want to clear ALL progress? This cannot be undone!')){ return; } allProblems.forEach(p => { p.cleaned = false; p.answer = ''; p.cleanedQuestion = p.q; }); localStorage.removeItem('uilCleanupProgress'); updateStats(); applyFilters(); showMessage('üóëÔ∏è All progress cleared', 'success'); } function showMessage(msg, type){ const el = document.getElementById('save-message'); el.className = 'save-indicator ' + (type === 'success' ? 'save-success' : 'save-error'); el.textContent = msg; el.style.display = 'block'; setTimeout(() => el.style.display = 'none', 3000); } // Keyboard shortcuts document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 's'){ e.preventDefault(); saveProblem(); } if((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'ArrowRight'){ e.preventDefault(); skipProblem(); } });
